In [3]:
def check_data(user_specified_files):
    for file_name in user_specified_files.split(' '):
        file = h5py.File(file_name, "r")
        count = 0
        for key in file.keys():
            if key[-9:] != "_metadata":
                print(key + ' has shape '+ str(np.array(file[key]).shape) + ' and type ' + str(file[key].dtype))
                count += 1
        print('there are ' + str(count) + 'image files')
        file.close()

# combined-images_XR-marked.hdf5
files = str(input("Enter file names to check, separating them by SPACES (i.e. file_1 file_2 file_3): "))
check_data(files)

LABELS = 'combined-images_XR-marked.hdf5'
labels = h5py.File(LABELS,'r')
inl = np.array(labels['Tibyey_ser_1_im_0']).astype('float32')
INDIMS = labels['Tibyey_ser_1_im_0'].shape # since not all CXRs are same size, have to zoom each by different ratio
ratio = float(256 / INDIMS[0])
ratio1 = float(256 / INDIMS[1])
inl = ndimage.zoom(inl, (ratio, ratio1,1,1), order=1)
inl = (inl - np.min(inl))/(np.max(inl) - np.min(inl))
inl = np.squeeze(inl) 
inl = inl[:,:,0:-1] 
plt.figure()
plt.imshow(inl[:,:,1],cmap='gray')
